<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="211" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="218" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}" class="Module">plfa.Adequacy</a> <a id="232" class="Keyword">where</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## Introduction

Having proved a preservation property in the last chapter, a natural
next step would be to prove progress. That is, to prove a property
of the form

    If γ ⊢ M ↓ v, then either M is a lambda abstraction or M —→ N for some N.

Such a property would tell us that having a denotation implies either
reduction to normal form or divergence. This is indeed true, but we
can prove a much stronger property! In fact, having a denotation that
is a function value (not `⊥`) implies reduction to a lambda
abstraction (no divergence).

This stronger property, reformulated a bit, is known as _adequacy_.
That is, if a term `M` is denotationally equal to a lambda abstraction,
then `M` reduces to a lambda abstraction.

    ℰ M ≃ ℰ (ƛ N)  implies M —↠ ƛ N' for some N'

Recall that `ℰ M ≃ ℰ (ƛ N)` is equivalent to saying that
`γ ⊢ M ↓ (v ↦ w)` for some `v` and `w`. We will show that
`γ ⊢ M ↓ (v ↦ w)` implies reduction a lambda abstraction.

It is well known that a term can reduce to a lambda abstraction using
full β reduction if and only if it can reduce to a lambda abstraction
using the call-by-name reduction strategy. So we shall prove that
`γ ⊢ M ↓ (v ↦ w)` implies that `M` halts under call-by-name evaluation,
which we define with a big-step semantics written `γ' ⊢ M ⇓ c`, where
`c` is a closure (a term paired with an environment) and `γ'` is an
environment that maps variables to closures

So we will show that `γ ⊢ M ↓ (v ↦ w)` implies `γ' ⊢ M ⇓ c`,
provided `γ` and `γ'` are appropriate related.  The proof will
be an induction on the derivation of `γ ⊢ M ↓ v`, and to
strengthen the induction hypothesis, we will relate semantic values to
closures using a _logical relation_ `𝕍`.

The rest of this chapter is organized as follows.

* We loosen the requirement that `M` result in a function value and
  instead require that `M` result in a value that is greater than or
  equal to a function value. We establish several properties about
  being ``greater than a function''.

* We define the call-by-name big-step semantics of the lambda calculus
  and prove that it is deterministic.

* We define the logical relation `𝕍` that relates values and closures,
  and extend it to a relation on terms `𝔼` and environments `𝔾`.

* We prove the main lemma,
  that if `𝔾 γ γ'` and `γ ⊢ M ↓ v`, then `𝔼 v (clos M γ')`.

* We prove adequacy as a corollary to the main lemma.

<a id="3659" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="3664" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="3671" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Relation.Nullary.html" class="Module">Relation.Nullary</a> <a id="3688" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="3694" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3695" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Relation.Nullary.html#464" class="Function Operator">¬_</a><a id="3697" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="3759" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="3764" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="3771" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Empty.html" class="Module">Data.Empty</a> <a id="3782" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="3788" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3789" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Empty.html#360" class="Function">⊥-elim</a><a id="3795" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3797" class="Keyword">renaming</a> <a id="3806" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3807" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Empty.html#243" class="Datatype">⊥</a> <a id="3809" class="Symbol">to</a> <a id="3812" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Empty.html#243" class="Datatype">Bot</a><a id="3815" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="3817" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="3822" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="3829" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Unit.html" class="Module">Data.Unit</a>

## The property of being greater or equal to a function

We define the following short-hand for saying that a value is
greather-than or equal to a function value.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="AboveFun"></a><a id="4112" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4112" class="Function">AboveFun</a> <a id="4121" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4123" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4000" class="Datatype">Value</a> <a id="4129" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4131" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a>
<a id="4135" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4112" class="Function">AboveFun</a> <a id="4144" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4144" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="4146" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="4148" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Product.html#764" class="Function">Σ[</a> <a id="4151" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4151" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="4153" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Product.html#764" class="Function">∈</a> <a id="4155" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4000" class="Datatype">Value</a> <a id="4161" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Product.html#764" class="Function">]</a> <a id="4163" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Product.html#764" class="Function">Σ[</a> <a id="4166" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4166" class="Bound">w</a> <a id="4168" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Product.html#764" class="Function">∈</a> <a id="4170" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4000" class="Datatype">Value</a> <a id="4176" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Product.html#764" class="Function">]</a> <a id="4178" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4151" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="4180" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4032" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">↦</a> <a id="4182" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4166" class="Bound">w</a> <a id="4184" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4371" class="Datatype Operator">⊑</a> <a id="4186" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4144" class="Bound">u</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

If a value `u` is greater than a function, then an even greater value `u'`
is too.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="AboveFun-⊑"></a><a id="4297" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4297" class="Function">AboveFun-⊑</a> <a id="4308" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4310" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="4312" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4312" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="4314" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4314" class="Bound">u&#39;</a> <a id="4317" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4319" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4000" class="Datatype">Value</a><a id="4324" class="Symbol">}</a>
      <a id="4332" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4334" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4112" class="Function">AboveFun</a> <a id="4343" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4312" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="4345" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4347" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4312" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="4349" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4371" class="Datatype Operator">⊑</a> <a id="4351" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4314" class="Bound">u&#39;</a>
        <a id="4362" class="Comment">-------------------</a>
      <a id="4388" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4390" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4112" class="Function">AboveFun</a> <a id="4399" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4314" class="Bound">u&#39;</a>

The bottom value `⊥` is not greater than a function.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="AboveFun⊥"></a><a id="4547" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4547" class="Function">AboveFun⊥</a> <a id="4557" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4559" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Relation.Nullary.html#464" class="Function Operator">¬</a> <a id="4561" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4112" class="Function">AboveFun</a> <a id="4570" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4020" class="InductiveConstructor">⊥</a>
<a id="4572" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4547" class="Function">AboveFun⊥</a> <a id="4582" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="4584" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4584" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="4586" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="4588" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="4590" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4590" class="Bound">w</a> <a id="4592" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="4594" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4594" class="Bound">lt</a> <a id="4597" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a> <a id="4599" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a>

    <a id="4716" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="4721" class="Bound">Γ⊆⊥</a> <a id="4725" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4706" class="Bound">m</a>
<a id="4727" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="4731" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="4733" class="Symbol">()</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

If the join of two values `u` and `u'` is greater than a function, then
at least one of them is too.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="AboveFun-⊔"></a><a id="4863" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4863" class="Function">AboveFun-⊔</a> <a id="4874" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4876" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="4878" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4878" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="4880" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4880" class="Bound">u&#39;</a><a id="4882" class="Symbol">}</a>
           <a id="4895" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4897" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4112" class="Function">AboveFun</a> <a id="4906" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4907" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4878" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="4909" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4062" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⊔</a> <a id="4911" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4880" class="Bound">u&#39;</a><a id="4913" class="Symbol">)</a>
           <a id="4926" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4928" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4112" class="Function">AboveFun</a> <a id="4937" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4878" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="4939" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Sum.Base.html#419" class="Datatype Operator">⊎</a> <a id="4941" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4112" class="Function">AboveFun</a> <a id="4950" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4880" class="Bound">u&#39;</a>

On the other hand, if neither of `u` and `u'` is greater than a function,
then their join is also not greater than a function.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="not-AboveFun-⊔"></a><a id="5376" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5376" class="Function">not-AboveFun-⊔</a> <a id="5391" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5393" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="5395" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5395" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="5397" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5397" class="Bound">u&#39;</a> <a id="5400" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5402" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4000" class="Datatype">Value</a><a id="5407" class="Symbol">}</a>
               <a id="5424" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5426" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Relation.Nullary.html#464" class="Function Operator">¬</a> <a id="5428" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4112" class="Function">AboveFun</a> <a id="5437" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5395" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="5439" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5441" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Relation.Nullary.html#464" class="Function Operator">¬</a> <a id="5443" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4112" class="Function">AboveFun</a> <a id="5452" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5397" class="Bound">u&#39;</a>
               <a id="5470" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5472" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Relation.Nullary.html#464" class="Function Operator">¬</a> <a id="5474" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4112" class="Function">AboveFun</a> <a id="5483" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5484" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5395" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="5486" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4062" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⊔</a> <a id="5488" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5397" class="Bound">u&#39;</a><a id="5490" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="5492" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5376" class="Function">not-AboveFun-⊔</a> <a id="5507" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5507" class="Bound">naf1</a> <a id="5512" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5512" class="Bound">naf2</a> <a id="5517" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5517" class="Bound">af12</a>
    <a id="5526" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="5531" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4863" class="Function">AboveFun-⊔</a> <a id="5542" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5517" class="Bound">af12</a>
<a id="5547" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="5551" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="5553" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Sum.Base.html#475" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₁</a> <a id="5558" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5558" class="Bound">af1</a> <a id="5562" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="5564" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Relation.Nullary.Negation.html#560" class="Function">contradiction</a> <a id="5578" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5558" class="Bound">af1</a> <a id="5582" class="Bound">naf1</a>
<a id="5587" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="5591" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="5593" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Sum.Base.html#500" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₂</a> <a id="5598" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5598" class="Bound">af2</a> <a id="5602" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="5604" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Relation.Nullary.Negation.html#560" class="Function">contradiction</a> <a id="5618" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5598" class="Bound">af2</a> <a id="5622" class="Bound">naf2</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

The converse is also true. If the join of two values is not above a
function, then neither of them is individually.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="not-AboveFun-⊔-inv"></a><a id="5769" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5769" class="Function">not-AboveFun-⊔-inv</a> <a id="5788" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5790" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="5792" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5792" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="5794" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5794" class="Bound">u&#39;</a> <a id="5797" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5799" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4000" class="Datatype">Value</a><a id="5804" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5806" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5808" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Relation.Nullary.html#464" class="Function Operator">¬</a> <a id="5810" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4112" class="Function">AboveFun</a> <a id="5819" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5820" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5792" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="5822" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4062" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⊔</a> <a id="5824" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5794" class="Bound">u&#39;</a><a id="5826" class="Symbol">)</a>
              <a id="5842" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5844" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Relation.Nullary.html#464" class="Function Operator">¬</a> <a id="5846" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4112" class="Function">AboveFun</a> <a id="5855" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5792" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="5857" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Product.html#1353" class="Function Operator">×</a> <a id="5859" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Relation.Nullary.html#464" class="Function Operator">¬</a> <a id="5861" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4112" class="Function">AboveFun</a> <a id="5870" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5794" class="Bound">u&#39;</a>

The property of being greater than a function value is decidable, as
exhibited by the following function.

## Relating values to closures

Next we relate semantic values to closures.  The relation `𝕍` is for
closures whose term is a lambda abstraction, i.e., in weak-head normal
form (WHNF). The relation 𝔼 is for any closure. Roughly speaking,
`𝔼 v c` will hold if, when `v` is greater than a function value, `c` evaluates
to a closure `c'` in WHNF and `𝕍 v c'`. Regarding `𝕍 v c`, it will hold when
`c` is in WHNF, and if `v` is a function, the body of `c` evaluates
according to `v`.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="𝕍"></a><a id="7223" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7223" class="Function">𝕍</a> <a id="7225" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7227" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4000" class="Datatype">Value</a> <a id="7233" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7235" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2452" class="Datatype">Clos</a> <a id="7240" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7242" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a>
<a id="𝔼"></a><a id="7246" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7246" class="Function">𝔼</a> <a id="7248" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7250" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4000" class="Datatype">Value</a> <a id="7256" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7258" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2452" class="Datatype">Clos</a> <a id="7263" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7265" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

We define `𝕍` as a function from values and closures to `Set` and not as a
data type because it is mutually recursive with `𝔼` in a negative
position (to the left of an implication).  We first perform case
analysis on the term in the closure. If the term is a variable or
application, then `𝕍` is false (`Bot`). If the term is a lambda
abstraction, we define `𝕍` by recursion on the value, which we
describe below.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="7710" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7223" class="Function">𝕍</a> <a id="7712" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7712" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="7714" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7715" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2471" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="7720" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7721" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4186" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`</a> <a id="7723" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7723" class="Bound">x₁</a><a id="7725" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7727" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7727" class="Bound">γ</a><a id="7728" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7730" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7732" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Empty.html#243" class="Datatype">Bot</a>
<a id="7736" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7223" class="Function">𝕍</a> <a id="7738" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7738" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="7740" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7741" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2471" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="7746" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7747" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7747" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="7749" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4298" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">·</a> <a id="7751" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7751" class="Bound">M₁</a><a id="7753" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7755" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7755" class="Bound">γ</a><a id="7756" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7758" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7760" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Empty.html#243" class="Datatype">Bot</a>

    <a id="7818" class="Symbol">(∀{</a><a id="7821" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7821" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="7823" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7825" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2452" class="Datatype">Clos</a><a id="7829" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7831" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7833" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7246" class="Function">𝔼</a> <a id="7835" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7790" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="7837" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7821" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="7839" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7841" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4112" class="Function">AboveFun</a> <a id="7850" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7794" class="Bound">w</a> <a id="7852" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7854" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Product.html#764" class="Function">Σ[</a> <a id="7857" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7857" class="Bound">c&#39;</a> <a id="7860" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Product.html#764" class="Function">∈</a> <a id="7862" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2452" class="Datatype">Clos</a> <a id="7867" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Product.html#764" class="Function">]</a>
        <a id="7877" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7878" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7809" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="7880" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2673" class="Function Operator">,&#39;</a> <a id="7883" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7821" class="Bound">c</a><a id="7884" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7886" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#3038" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="7888" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7806" class="Bound">N</a> <a id="7890" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#3038" class="Datatype Operator">⇓</a> <a id="7892" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7857" class="Bound">c&#39;</a>  <a id="7896" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Product.html#1353" class="Function Operator">×</a>  <a id="7899" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7223" class="Function">𝕍</a> <a id="7901" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7794" class="Bound">w</a> <a id="7903" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7857" class="Bound">c&#39;</a><a id="7905" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="7907" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7223" class="Function">𝕍</a> <a id="7909" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7910" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7910" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="7912" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4062" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⊔</a> <a id="7914" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7914" class="Bound">v</a><a id="7915" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7917" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7918" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2471" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="7923" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7924" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4238" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ</a> <a id="7926" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7926" class="Bound">N</a><a id="7927" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7929" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7929" class="Bound">γ</a><a id="7930" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7932" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7934" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7223" class="Function">𝕍</a> <a id="7936" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7910" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="7938" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7939" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2471" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="7944" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7945" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4238" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ</a> <a id="7947" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7926" class="Bound">N</a><a id="7948" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7950" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7929" class="Bound">γ</a><a id="7951" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7953" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Product.html#1353" class="Function Operator">×</a> <a id="7955" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7223" class="Function">𝕍</a> <a id="7957" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7914" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="7959" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7960" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2471" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="7965" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7966" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4238" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ</a> <a id="7968" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7926" class="Bound">N</a><a id="7969" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7971" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7929" class="Bound">γ</a><a id="7972" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

* If the value is `⊥`, then the result is true (`⊤`).

* If the value is a join (u ⊔ v), then the result is the pair
  (conjunction) of 𝕍 is true for both u and v.

* The important case is for a function value `v ↦ w` and closure
  `clos (ƛ N) γ`. Given any closure `c` such that `𝔼 v c`, if `w` is
  greater than a function, then `N` evaluates (with `γ` extended with `c`)
  to some closure `c'` and we have `𝕍 w c'`.


The definition of `𝔼` is straightforward. If `v` is a greater than a
function, then `M` evaluates to a closure related to `v`.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="8548" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7246" class="Function">𝔼</a> <a id="8550" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8560" class="Bound">γ&#39;</a><a id="8562" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8564" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8566" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4112" class="Function">AboveFun</a> <a id="8575" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8550" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="8577" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8579" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Product.html#764" class="Function">Σ[</a> <a id="8582" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8582" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="8584" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Product.html#764" class="Function">∈</a> <a id="8586" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2452" class="Datatype">Clos</a> <a id="8591" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Product.html#764" class="Function">]</a> <a id="8593" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8560" class="Bound">γ&#39;</a> <a id="8596" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#3038" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="8598" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8558" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="8600" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#3038" class="Datatype Operator">⇓</a> <a id="8602" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8582" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="8604" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Product.html#1353" class="Function Operator">×</a> <a id="8606" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7223" class="Function">𝕍</a> <a id="8608" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8550" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="8610" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8582" class="Bound">c</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

The proof of the main lemma is by induction on `γ ⊢ M ↓ v`, so it goes
underneath lambda abstractions and must therefore reason about open
terms (terms with variables). So we must relate environments of
semantic values to environments of closures.  In the following, `𝔾`
relates `γ` to `γ'` if the corresponding values and closures are related
by `𝔼`.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="𝔾"></a><a id="8990" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8990" class="Function">𝔾</a> <a id="8992" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8994" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="8996" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8996" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="8997" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="8999" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9001" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#7234" class="Function">Env</a> <a id="9005" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8996" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="9007" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9009" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2422" class="Function">ClosEnv</a> <a id="9017" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8996" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="9019" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9021" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a>
<a id="9025" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8990" class="Function">𝔾</a> <a id="9027" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9028" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9028" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="9029" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9031" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9031" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="9033" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9033" class="Bound">γ&#39;</a> <a id="9036" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9038" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="9040" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9040" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="9042" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9044" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9028" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="9046" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3365" class="Datatype Operator">∋</a> <a id="9048" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a><a id="9049" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9051" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9053" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7246" class="Function">𝔼</a> <a id="9055" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9056" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9031" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="9058" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9040" class="Bound">x</a><a id="9059" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9061" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9062" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9033" class="Bound">γ&#39;</a> <a id="9065" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9040" class="Bound">x</a><a id="9066" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="𝔾-∅"></a><a id="9069" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9069" class="Function">𝔾-∅</a> <a id="9073" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9075" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8990" class="Function">𝔾</a> <a id="9077" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#7374" class="Function">`∅</a> <a id="9080" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2651" class="Function">∅&#39;</a>

      <a id="9144" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9146" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8990" class="Function">𝔾</a> <a id="9148" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9106" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="9150" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9117" class="Bound">γ&#39;</a> <a id="9153" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9155" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7246" class="Function">𝔼</a> <a id="9157" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9133" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="9159" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9135" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="9161" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9163" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8990" class="Function">𝔾</a> <a id="9165" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9166" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9106" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="9168" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#7407" class="Function Operator">`,</a> <a id="9171" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9133" class="Bound">v</a><a id="9172" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9174" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9175" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9117" class="Bound">γ&#39;</a> <a id="9178" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2673" class="Function Operator">,&#39;</a> <a id="9181" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9135" class="Bound">c</a><a id="9182" class="Symbol">)</a>

We need a few properties of the `𝕍` and `𝔼` relations.  The first is that
a closure in the `𝕍` relation must be in weak-head normal form.  We
define WHNF has follows.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="9442" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="WHNF"></a><a id="9447" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9447" class="Datatype">WHNF</a> <a id="9452" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9454" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="9456" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9457" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9457" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="9459" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9459" class="Bound">A</a><a id="9460" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9462" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9464" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9457" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="9466" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4150" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="9468" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9459" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="9470" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9472" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="9476" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="WHNF.ƛ_"></a><a id="9484" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9484" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ_</a> <a id="9487" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9489" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="9491" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9492" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9492" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="9493" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9495" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9496" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9496" class="Bound">N</a> <a id="9498" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9500" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9492" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="9502" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3018" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="9504" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a> <a id="9506" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4150" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="9508" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a><a id="9509" class="Symbol">}</a>
     <a id="9516" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9518" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9447" class="Datatype">WHNF</a> <a id="9523" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9524" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4238" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ</a> <a id="9526" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9496" class="Bound">N</a><a id="9527" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

The proof goes by cases on the term in the closure.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="𝕍→WHNF"></a><a id="9607" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9607" class="Function">𝕍→WHNF</a> <a id="9614" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9616" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="9618" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9618" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="9619" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="9621" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9621" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="9623" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9625" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2422" class="Function">ClosEnv</a> <a id="9633" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9618" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="9634" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="9636" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9636" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="9638" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9640" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9618" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="9642" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4150" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="9644" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a><a id="9645" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="9647" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9647" class="Bound">v</a><a id="9648" class="Symbol">}</a>
       <a id="9657" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9659" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7223" class="Function">𝕍</a> <a id="9661" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9647" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="9663" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9664" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2471" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="9669" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9636" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="9671" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9621" class="Bound">γ</a><a id="9672" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9674" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9676" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9447" class="Datatype">WHNF</a> <a id="9681" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9636" class="Bound">M</a>
<a id="9683" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9607" class="Function">𝕍→WHNF</a> <a id="9690" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9691" class="Argument">M</a> <a id="9693" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9695" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4186" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`</a> <a id="9697" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9697" class="Bound">x</a><a id="9698" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9700" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9701" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9701" class="Bound">v</a><a id="9702" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9704" class="Symbol">()</a>
<a id="9707" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9607" class="Function">𝕍→WHNF</a> <a id="9714" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9715" class="Argument">M</a> <a id="9717" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9719" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4238" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ</a> <a id="9721" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9721" class="Bound">N</a><a id="9722" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9724" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9725" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9725" class="Bound">v</a><a id="9726" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9728" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9728" class="Bound">vc</a> <a id="9731" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9733" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9484" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ_</a>
<a id="9736" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9607" class="Function">𝕍→WHNF</a> <a id="9743" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9744" class="Argument">M</a> <a id="9746" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9748" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9748" class="Bound">L</a> <a id="9750" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4298" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">·</a> <a id="9752" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9752" class="Bound">M</a><a id="9753" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9755" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9756" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9756" class="Bound">v</a><a id="9757" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9759" class="Symbol">()</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Next we have an introduction rule for `𝕍` that mimics the `⊔-intro`
rule. If both `u` and `v` are related to a closure `c`, then their join is
too.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="𝕍⊔-intro"></a><a id="9936" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9936" class="Function">𝕍⊔-intro</a> <a id="9945" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9947" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="9949" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9949" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="9951" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9951" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="9953" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9953" class="Bound">v</a><a id="9954" class="Symbol">}</a>
         <a id="9965" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9967" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7223" class="Function">𝕍</a> <a id="9969" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9951" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="9971" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9949" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="9973" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9975" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7223" class="Function">𝕍</a> <a id="9977" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9953" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="9979" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9949" class="Bound">c</a>
           <a id="9992" class="Comment">---------------</a>
         <a id="10017" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10019" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7223" class="Function">𝕍</a> <a id="10021" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10022" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9951" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="10024" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4062" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⊔</a> <a id="10026" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9953" class="Bound">v</a><a id="10027" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10029" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9949" class="Bound">c</a>
<a id="10031" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9936" class="Function">𝕍⊔-intro</a> <a id="10040" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10041" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2471" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="10046" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10047" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4186" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`</a> <a id="10049" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10049" class="Bound">x</a><a id="10050" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10052" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10052" class="Bound">γ</a><a id="10053" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="10055" class="Symbol">()</a> <a id="10058" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10058" class="Bound">vc</a>
<a id="10061" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9936" class="Function">𝕍⊔-intro</a> <a id="10070" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10071" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2471" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="10076" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10077" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4238" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ</a> <a id="10079" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10079" class="Bound">N</a><a id="10080" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10082" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10082" class="Bound">γ</a><a id="10083" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="10085" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10085" class="Bound">uc</a> <a id="10088" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10088" class="Bound">vc</a> <a id="10091" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10093" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="10095" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10085" class="Bound">uc</a> <a id="10098" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="10100" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10088" class="Bound">vc</a> <a id="10103" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a>
<a id="10105" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9936" class="Function">𝕍⊔-intro</a> <a id="10114" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10115" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2471" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="10120" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10121" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10121" class="Bound">L</a> <a id="10123" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4298" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">·</a> <a id="10125" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10125" class="Bound">M</a><a id="10126" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10128" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10128" class="Bound">γ</a><a id="10129" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="10131" class="Symbol">()</a> <a id="10134" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10134" class="Bound">vc</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

In a moment we prove that `𝕍` is preserved when going from a greater
value to a lesser value: if `𝕍 v c` and `v' ⊑ v`, then `𝕍 v' c`.
This property, named `𝕍-sub`, is needed by the main lemma in
the case for the `sub` rule.

To prove `𝕍-sub`, we in turn need the following property concerning
values that are not greater than a function, that is, values that are
equivalent to `⊥`. In such cases, `𝕍 v (clos (ƛ N) γ')` is trivially true.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="not-AboveFun-𝕍"></a><a id="10601" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10601" class="Function">not-AboveFun-𝕍</a> <a id="10616" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10618" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="10620" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10620" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="10622" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10624" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4000" class="Datatype">Value</a><a id="10629" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="10631" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10631" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="10632" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="10634" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10634" class="Bound">γ&#39;</a> <a id="10637" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10639" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2422" class="Function">ClosEnv</a> <a id="10647" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10631" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="10648" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="10650" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10650" class="Bound">N</a> <a id="10652" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10654" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10631" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="10656" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3018" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="10658" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a> <a id="10660" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4150" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="10662" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a> <a id="10664" class="Symbol">}</a>
    <a id="10670" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10672" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Relation.Nullary.html#464" class="Function Operator">¬</a> <a id="10674" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4112" class="Function">AboveFun</a> <a id="10683" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10620" class="Bound">v</a>
      <a id="10691" class="Comment">-------------------</a>
    <a id="10715" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10717" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7223" class="Function">𝕍</a> <a id="10719" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10620" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="10721" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10722" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2471" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="10727" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10728" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4238" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ</a> <a id="10730" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10650" class="Bound">N</a><a id="10731" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10733" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10634" class="Bound">γ&#39;</a><a id="10735" class="Symbol">)</a>

The proofs of `𝕍-sub` and `𝔼-sub` are intertwined.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="sub-𝕍"></a><a id="11044" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11044" class="Function">sub-𝕍</a> <a id="11050" endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4371" class="Datatype Operator">⊑</a> <a id="11137" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11116" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="11139" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11141" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7246" class="Function">𝔼</a> <a id="11143" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11118" class="Bound">v&#39;</a> <a id="11146" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11106" class="Bound">c</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

We prove `𝕍-sub` by case analysis on the closure's term, to dispatch the
cases for variables and application. We then proceed by induction on
`v' ⊑ v`. We describe each case below.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="11355" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11044" class="Function">sub-𝕍</a> <a id="11361" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="11362" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2471" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="11367" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11368" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4186" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`</a> <a id="11370" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11370" class="Bound">x</a><a id="11371" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11373" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11373" class="Bound">γ</a><a id="11374" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="11376" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="11377" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11377" class="Bound">v</a><a id="11378" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="11380" class="Symbol">()</a> <a id="11383" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11383" class="Bound">lt</a>

    <a id="12901" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="12906" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4863" class="Function">AboveFun-⊔</a> <a id="12917" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="12919" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#12853" class="Bound">v&#39;</a> <a id="12922" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="12924" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="12926" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#12860" class="Bound">w&#39;&#39;</a> <a id="12930" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="12932" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#12866" class="Bound">lt</a> <a id="12935" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a> <a id="12937" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a>
<a id="12939" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="12943" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="12945" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Sum.Base.html#475" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₁</a> <a id="12950" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#12950" class="Bound">af2</a> <a id="12954" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="12956" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Empty.html#360" class="Function">⊥-elim</a> <a id="12963" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12964" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Relation.Nullary.Negation.html#560" class="Function">contradiction</a> <a id="12978" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#12950" class="Bound">af2</a> <a id="12982" class="Bound">naf2</a><a id="12986" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="12988" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="12992" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="12994" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Sum.Base.html#500" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₂</a> <a id="12999" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#12999" class="Bound">af3</a> <a id="13003" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13005" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Empty.html#360" class="Function">⊥-elim</a> <a id="13012" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13013" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Relation.Nullary.Negation.html#560" class="Function">contradiction</a> <a id="13027" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#12999" class="Bound">af3</a> <a id="13031" class="Bound">naf3</a><a id="13035" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

* Case `Bot⊑`. We immediately have `𝕍 ⊥ (clos (ƛ N) γ)`.

* Case `ConjL⊑`.

        v₁' ⊑ v     v₂' ⊑ v
        -------------------
        (v₁' ⊔ v₂') ⊑ v

  The induction hypotheses gives us `𝕍 v₁' (clos (ƛ N) γ)`
  and `𝕍 v₂' (clos (ƛ N) γ)`, which is all we need for this case. 

* Case `ConjR1⊑`.

        v' ⊑ v₁
        -------------
        v' ⊑ (v₁ ⊔ v₂)

  The induction hypothesis gives us `𝕍 v' (clos (ƛ N) γ)`.

* Case `ConjR2⊑`.

        v' ⊑ v₂
        -------------
        v' ⊑ (v₁ ⊔ v₂)

  Again, the induction hypothesis gives us `𝕍 v' (clos (ƛ N) γ)`.

* Case `Trans⊑`.

        v' ⊑ v₂   v₂ ⊑ v
        -----------------
             v' ⊑ v

  The induction hypothesis for `v₂ ⊑ v` gives us
  `𝕍 v₂ (clos (ƛ N) γ)`. We apply the induction hypothesis
  for `v' ⊑ v₂` to conclude that `𝕍 v' (clos (ƛ N) γ)`.

* Case `Dist⊑`. This case  is the most difficult. We have

        𝕍 (v ↦ w) (clos (ƛ N) γ)
        𝕍 (v ↦ w') (clos (ƛ N) γ)

  and need to show that 

        𝕍 (v ↦ (w ⊔ w')) (clos (ƛ N) γ)
  
  Let `c` be an arbtrary closure such that `𝔼 v c`.
  Assume `w ⊔ w'` is greater than a function.
  Unfortunately, this does not mean that both `w` and `w'`
  are above functions. But thanks to the lemma `AboveFun-⊔`,
  we know that at least one of them is greater than a function.
  
  * Suppose both of them are greater than a function.  Then we have
    `γ ⊢ N ⇓ clos L δ` and `𝕍 w (clos L δ)`.  We also have `γ ⊢ N ⇓ c₃` and
    `𝕍 w' c₃`.  Because the big-step semantics is deterministic, we have
    `c₃ ≡ clos L δ`. Also, from `𝕍 w (clos L δ)` we know that `L ≡ ƛ N'`
    for some `N'`. We conclude that `𝕍 (w ⊔ w') (clos (ƛ N') δ)`.

  * Suppose one of them is greater than a function and the other is
    not: say `AboveFun w` and `¬ AboveFun w'`. Then from
    `𝕍 (v ↦ w) (clos (ƛ N) γ)`
    we have `γ ⊢ N ⇓ clos L γ₁` and `𝕍 w (clos L γ₁)`. From this we have
    `L ≡ ƛ N'` for some `N'`. Meanwhile, from `¬ AboveFun w'` we have
    `𝕍 w' (clos L γ₁)`. We conclude that
    `𝕍 (w ⊔ w') (clos (ƛ N') γ₁)`.
    

The proof of `sub-𝔼` is direct and explained below.

    <a id="15204" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="15209" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#15188" class="Bound">𝔼v</a> <a id="15212" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15213" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4297" class="Function">AboveFun-⊑</a> <a id="15224" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#15196" class="Bound">fv&#39;</a> <a id="15228" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#15191" class="Bound">v&#39;⊑v</a><a id="15232" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="15234" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="15238" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="15240" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="15242" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#15242" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="15244" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="15246" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="15248" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#15248" class="Bound">M⇓c</a> <a id="15252" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="15254" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#15254" class="Bound">𝕍v</a> <a id="15257" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a> <a id="15259" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a> <a id="15261" class="Symbol">=</a>
      <a id="15269" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="15271" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#15242" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="15273" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="15275" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="15277" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#15248" class="Bound">M⇓c</a> <a id="15281" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="15283" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11044" class="Function">sub-𝕍</a> <a id="15289" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#15254" class="Bound">𝕍v</a> <a id="15292" class="Bound">v&#39;⊑v</a> <a id="15297" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a> <a id="15299" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

From `AboveFun v'` and `v' ⊑ v` we have `AboveFun v`.  Then with `𝔼 v c` we
obtain a closure `c` such that `γ ⊢ M ⇓ c` and `𝕍 v c`. We conclude with an
application of `sub-𝕍` with `v' ⊑ v` to show `𝕍 v' c`.


## Programs with function denotation terminate via call-by-name

The main lemma proves that if a term has a denotation that is above a
function, then it terminates via call-by-name. More formally, if
`γ ⊢ M ↓ v` and `𝔾 γ γ'`, then `𝔼 v (clos M γ')`. The proof is by
induction on the derivation of `γ ⊢ M ↓ v` we discuss each case below.

The following lemma, kth-x, is used in the case for the `var` rule.

      <a id="18298" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="18300" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#18271" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="18302" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="18304" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="18306" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#18277" class="Bound">M⇓c</a> <a id="18310" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="18312" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11044" class="Function">sub-𝕍</a> <a id="18318" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#18283" class="Bound">𝕍v</a> <a id="18321" class="Bound">v&#39;⊑v</a> <a id="18326" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a> <a id="18328" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

* Case `var`. Looking up `x` in `γ'` yields some closure, `clos M' δ`,
  and from `𝔾 γ γ'` we have `𝔼 (γ x) (clos M' δ)`. With the premise
  `AboveFun (γ x)`, we obtain a closure `c` such that `δ ⊢ M' ⇓ c`
  and `𝕍 (γ x) c`. To conclude `γ' ⊢ x ⇓ c` via `⇓-var`, we 
  need `γ' x ≡ clos M' δ`, which is obvious, but it requires some
  Agda shananigans via the `kth-x` lemma to get our hands on it.

* Case `↦-elim`. We have `γ ⊢ L · M ↓ v`.
  The induction hypothesis for `γ ⊢ L ↓ v₁ ↦ v`
  gives us `γ' ⊢ L ⇓ clos L' δ` and `𝕍 v (clos L' δ)`.
  Of course, `L' ≡ ƛ N` for some `N`.
  By the induction hypothesis for `γ ⊢ M ↓ v₁`,
  we have `𝔼 v₁ (clos M γ')`.
  Together with the premise `AboveFun v` and `𝕍 v (clos L' δ)`,
  we obtain a closure `c'` such that `δ ⊢ N ⇓ c'` and `𝕍 v c'`.
  We conclude that `γ' ⊢ L · M ⇓ c'` by rule `⇓-app`.

* Case `↦-intro`. We have `γ ⊢ ƛ N ↓ v ↦ w`.
  We immediately have `γ' ⊢ ƛ M ⇓ clos (ƛ M) γ'` by rule `⇓-lam`.
  But we also need to prove `𝕍 (v ↦ w) (clos (ƛ N) γ')`.
  Let `c` by an arbitrary closure such that `𝔼 v c`.
  Suppose `v'` is greater than a function value.
  We need to show that `γ' , c ⊢ N ⇓ c'` and `𝕍 v' c'` for some `c'`.
  We prove this by the induction hypothesis for `γ , v ⊢ N ↓ v'`
  but we must first show that `𝔾 (γ , v) (γ' , c)`. We prove
  that by the lemma `𝔾-ext`, using facts `𝔾 γ γ'` and `𝔼 v c`.

* Case `⊥-intro`. We have the premise `AboveFun ⊥`, but that's impossible.

* Case `⊔-intro`. We have `γ ⊢ M ↓ (v₁ ⊔ v₂)` and `AboveFun (v₁ ⊔ v₂)`
  and need to show `γ' ⊢ M ↓ c` and `𝕍 (v₁ ⊔ v₂) c` for some `c`.
  Again, by `AboveFun-⊔`, at least one of `v₁` or `v₂` is greater than
  a function.

  * Suppose both `v₁` and `v₂` are greater than a function value.
    By the induction hypotheses for `γ ⊢ M ↓ v₁` and `γ ⊢ M ↓ v₂`
    we have `γ' ⊢ M ⇓ c₁`, `𝕍 v₁ c₁`, `γ' ⊢ M ⇓ c₂`, and `𝕍 v₂ c₂`
    for some `c₁` and `c₂`. Because `⇓` is deterministic, we have `c₂ ≡ c₁`.
    Then by `𝕍⊔-intro` we conclude that `𝕍 (v₁ ⊔ v₂) c₁`.

  * Without loss of generality, suppose `v₁` is greater than a function
    value but `v₂` is not.  By the induction hypotheses for `γ ⊢ M ↓ v₁`,
    and using `𝕍→WHNF`, we have `γ' ⊢ M ⇓ clos (ƛ N) γ₁`
    and `𝕍 v₁ (clos (ƛ N) γ₁)`.
    Then because `v₂` is not greater than a function, we also have
    `𝕍 v₂ (clos (ƛ N) γ₁)`. We conclude that `𝕍 (v₁ ⊔ v₂) (clos (ƛ N) γ₁)`.
    
* Case `sub`. We have `γ ⊢ M ↓ v`, `v' ⊑ v`, and `AboveFun v'`.
  We need to show that `γ' ⊢ M ⇓ c` and `𝕍 v' c` for some `c`.
  We have `AboveFun v` by `AboveFun-⊑`,
  so the induction hypothesis for `γ ⊢ M ↓ v` gives us a closure `c`
  such that `γ' ⊢ M ⇓ c` and `𝕍 v c`. We conclude that `𝕍 v' c` by `sub-𝕍`.


## Proof of denotational adequacy

The adequacy property is a corollary of the main lemma.
We have `∅ ⊢ ƛ N ↓ ⊥ ↦ ⊥`, so `ℰ M ≃ ℰ (ƛ N)`
gives us `∅ ⊢ M ↓ ⊥ ↦ ⊥`. Then the main lemma gives us
`∅ ⊢ M ⇓ clos (ƛ N′) γ` for some `N′` and `γ`.

            <a id="21438" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2651" class="Function">∅&#39;</a> <a id="21441" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#3038" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="21443" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#21312" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="21445" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#3038" class="Datatype Operator">⇓</a> <a id="21447" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2471" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="21452" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21453" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4238" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ</a> <a id="21455" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#21388" class="Bound">N′</a><a id="21457" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="21459" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#21410" class="Bound">γ</a>

    <a id="21622" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="21627" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9607" class="Function">𝕍→WHNF</a> <a id="21634" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#21611" class="Bound">Vc</a>

## Call-by-name is equivalent to beta reduction

As promised, we return to the question of whether call-by-name
evaluation is equivalent to beta reduction. In the chapter CallByName
we established the forward direction: that if call-by-name produces a
result, then the program beta reduces to a lambda abstraction.  We now
prove the backward direction of the if-and-only-if, leveraging our
results about the denotational semantics.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="reduce→cbn"></a><a id="22151" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#22151" class="Function">reduce→cbn</a> <a id="22162" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22164" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="22166" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="22167" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#22167" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="22169" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22171" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3002" class="InductiveConstructor">∅</a> <a id="22173" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4150" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="22175" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a><a id="22176" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="22178" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="22179" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#22179" class="Bound">N</a> <a id="22181" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22183" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3002" class="InductiveConstructor">∅</a> <a id="22185" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3018" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="22187" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a> <a id="22189" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4150" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="22191" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a><a id="22192" class="Symbol">}</a>
           <a id="22205" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="22207" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#22167" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="22209" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/LambdaReduction.md %}{% raw %}#894" class="Datatype Operator">—↠</a> <a id="22212" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4238" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ</a> <a id="22214" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#22179" class="Bound">N</a>

             <a id="22299" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2651" class="Function">∅&#39;</a> <a id="22302" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#3038" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="22304" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#22167" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="22306" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#3038" class="Datatype Operator">⇓</a> <a id="22308" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2471" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="22313" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="22314" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4238" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ</a> <a id="22316" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#22249" class="Bound">N′</a><a id="22318" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="22320" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#22269" class="Bound">δ</a>
<a id="22322" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#22151" class="Function">reduce→cbn</a> <a id="22333" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#22333" class="Bound">M—↠ƛN</a> <a id="22339" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="22341" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#21299" class="Function">adequacy</a> <a id="22350" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="22351" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Soundness.md %}{% raw %}#24047" class="Function">soundness</a> <a id="22361" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#22333" class="Bound">M—↠ƛN</a><a id="22366" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Suppose `M —↠ ƛ N`. Soundness of the denotational semantics gives us
`ℰ M ≃ ℰ (ƛ N)`. Then by adequacy we conclude that
`∅' ⊢ M ⇓ clos (ƛ N′) δ` for some `N′` and `δ`.

Putting the two directions of the if-and-only-if together, we
establish that call-by-name evaluation is equivalent to beta reduction
in the following sense.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="cbn↔reduce"></a><a id="22720" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#22720" class="Function">cbn↔reduce</a> <a id="22731" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22733" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="22735" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="22736" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#22736" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="22738" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22740" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3002" class="InductiveConstructor">∅</a> <a id="22742" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4150" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="22744" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a><a id="22745" class="Symbol">}</a>
